    E -->|not contains| H[skip]
    G --> I{location_set empty?}

    class Module_fv {
        +fetch_organization_granted_locations(event, dereference=True, given_org_id=None)
        +get_dda_visibility(cursor, data, dda_status=None, solution_id=None, entity_alias="e")
    }
    class fetch_organization_granted_locations {
        +calls invokinator_location.get_location_grants(event, dereference, grantee_id)
        +collects resolved_referent_id and child_ids into location_ids
    }
    class get_dda_visibility {
        +calls system_config.get_system_configuration_setting(...)
        +parses JSON entries for DDA_LOCATION_VISIBILITY
        +builds visibility_clause and sets data["dda_location_visibility_set"]
    }
    Module_fv <|-- fetch_organization_granted_locations
    Module_fv <|-- get_dda_visibility

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Caller as main / other code
    participant Module as fv module
    participant SystemConfig as system_config
    participant Invokinator as invokinator_location
    Caller->>Module: call fetch_organization_granted_locations(event)
    Module->>Invokinator: get_location_grants(event, dereference, grantee_id)
    Invokinator-->>Module: org_results
    Module-->>Caller: location_ids list
    Caller->>Module: call get_dda_visibility(cursor, data, solution_id)
    Module->>SystemConfig: get_system_configuration_setting(cursor, DDA_LOCATION_VISIBILITY, solution_id)
    SystemConfig-->>Module: location_ids
    Module-->>Module: parse JSON entries, build location_set
    Module->>Module: construct visibility_clause
    Module-->>Caller: return visibility_clause
```

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> Idle
    Idle --> FetchConfig: get_system_configuration_setting
    FetchConfig --> ParseEntries
    ParseEntries --> BuildSet
    BuildSet --> CheckEmpty
    CheckEmpty --> EmptyClause: location_set is empty
    CheckEmpty --> BuildClause: location_set not empty
    EmptyClause --> ReturnClause
    BuildClause --> SetDataAndReturn
    SetDataAndReturn --> ReturnClause
    ReturnClause --> [*]
```
